            </span>
           </div>
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>

        <div class="weather-bar" ng-controller="WeatherWidgetCtrl">
         <div class="dropdown">
          <button class="dropdown-toggle" data-toggle="dropdown" ng-cloak="" type="button">
           <i class="icon icon-weather">
           </i>
           <span>
            {$ currentCity.name $}
           </span>
           <i class="icon icon-angle-down">
           </i>
          </button>
          <div class="dropdown-menu">
           <div class="nano" cnn-custom-scroll="" data-height="256">
            <ul class="nano-content">
             <li id="{$::city.id$}" ng-class="{ 'active' : currentCity.name === city.name}" ng-mousedown="selectCity($index)" ng-repeat="city in cities track by $index" role="option">
              {$ city.name $}
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <a class="weather-value" href="{$ currentCity.link $}" ng-cloak="" ng-repeat="day in cityDays | limitTo : 1 : 1" target="_blank">
          <span>
           {$ day.Temps.HighTemp $}
          </span>
          <i class="degree">
           °
          </i>

       <h6 class="text-center">
        Dünyadan en son haberler, Türkiye'den son dakika gelişmeleri, günün öne çıkan gündem haberleri, dünya ekonomi piyasalarından flaş haberler, en yeni spor haberleri ve magazin dünyasından son olaylar CNN Türk'te.
